 Srinivasan will be the new chairman of the International Cricket Council (ICC)
 vahiin mustafa kamaal isisi ke nae adhyaksh honge
 Under the agenda, the amendment to the ICC constitution was approved on the fourth day of the conference on Thursday, which was agreed by the ICC Board in Singapore on 8 February
 melborn main hui baithak main shrinivasana kii chairman pad par niyukti kii pushti ho gai
 In this way, he will be the first chairman of the ICC
 singapore main hui baithak main liye gaye faislon main is par sahmati jataai gai thi ki isisi samvidhan main chairman kaa pad banaaya jayega
 Under this the amendment has been prepared but will be placed before the full council for approval before it is accepted
 bisisiai ne isisi board ke adhyaksh pad ke liye apane ummidavaar ke rup main shrinivasana kaa naam bheja tha
 a few days before the Supreme Court's refusal to stop n Srinivasan from assuming the post of Chairman, the BCCI has reaffirmed that Srinivasan will be the candidate for the post
 tamilnadu ke kaddavar khel prashaasak shrinivasana isi maah melbern main isisi board ke chairman kaa pad sanbhaalenge
 The ICC Council has 51 members of which 36 are Associate, five Affiliate and 10 Full Time Members
 inamen bharat, pakistan, australia, england, dakshin africa, newjiland, srilanka, bangladesh, zimbabwe or westeindies shaamil hai
 Srinivasan will take up the position after the annual conference ends on 28 June
 shrinivasana ko isisi chairman pad par kabiz hone se rokane ke liye amaanya bihar cricket sangh kii yachika par sunwaayee se ucchtam nyaayalay ke inkaar ke baad bisisiai ne shrinivasana ke naam kii phir pushti kii thi
 The board has also taken legal advice on the issue and the ICC has been informed that it would not be a contempt of court if Srinivasan holds the post of ICC chairman or represents BCCI in the ICC
 shrinivasana ne pichley maheene asian cricket parishad kii baithak kii adhyakshata bhi kii thi

 nehru kii patni kamala nehru khud swatantraaa senaanee thim
 Nehru's father Motilal Nehru was also a hero of independence
 nehru kii bahan vijay lakshmi pandit swatantraaa senaanee thim
 It was in Nehru's life that Indira Gandhi became Congress President in 1959
 1960 main neelam sanjeev reddy adhyaksh ban gaye the

 indira gandhi ko zyaada sabit karnaa padaa raajnneeti main
 Congress was formed
 haari or jitati raheen wo alag kahani he

 Sardar Patel's family has also been in politics
 vitthal bhai patel sardaar vallabh bhai patel ke sage bade bhai the

 vitthal bhai patel 1925 main central legislative asambeli ke adhyaksh or spikar the
 His younger brother Sardar Ballabh Bhai Patel became the Home Minister
 patel kii pahchaan vitthal bhai ke chote bhai se nahin, bardoli ke kisaan andolan se thi

 vivaad hone par nehru ne kaha ki ve beti hai magar 1930 se azaadi kii ladaai main shaamil hai
 Patel's daughter Maniben Patel and son Dayabhai Patel both contested the Lok Sabha elections in 1957
 baad main maniben patel rajya sabha kii sadsy bhi huin magar iske baad patel parivaar sunai nahin diya
 Today, the Patel family has no claim on that legacy
 unki koi party nahin he
 Lal Bahadur Shastri's family also came into politics but the sons of that honest and simple leader did not get any special political benefit
 jabaki ek congress main rahe or duusare bijepi main
 Biju Patnaik's son Naveen Patnaik is also an example

 Rahul Gandhi has been hesitant about this familyism for a long time, but now it seems that he has overcome this criticism, but this question will continue to follow him
